MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

I, C. Vasanthakumar natural son of Thiru. C. Venkatesan, residing at New No. 19, Old No. 10, 11th Cross Street,
Indira Nagar, Chennai-600 020. By way of the public notice, I inform that late M. Nandagopal has legally adopted
me as his son on date 29-5-2001 by way of registered deed number 678 of 2001 on the file of sub registrar of Ambattur,
Chennai-600 053. My adopted father late M. Nandagopal passed away on 26-6-2013, hereafter I shall be
known as N. VASANTHAKUMAR.
Chennai,
6th May 2016.

C. VASANTHAKUMAR,
